\subsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\hypertarget{_s_d_l__keysym_8h_ab8a13abddfa48bf4201973c2aa0afc1a}{\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-keysym.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-keysym.\-h}!S\-D\-L\-Key@{S\-D\-L\-Key}}
\index{S\-D\-L\-Key@{S\-D\-L\-Key}!SDL_keysym.h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-keysym.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{S\-D\-L\-Key}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf S\-D\-L\-Key}}}\label{_s_d_l__keysym_8h_ab8a13abddfa48bf4201973c2aa0afc1a}


The names of the keys. 

What we really want is a mapping of every raw key on the keyboard. To support international keyboards, we use the range 0x\-A1 -\/ 0x\-F\-F as international virtual keycodes. We'll follow in the footsteps of X11... \begin{Desc}
\item[Enumerator]\par
